# <a name="customize-service-fabric-cluster-settings-and-fabric-upgrade-policy"></a><span data-ttu-id="dc34a-103">Anpassa inställningar för Service Fabric-kluster och Fabric-uppgradera princip</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-103">Customize Service Fabric cluster settings and Fabric Upgrade policy</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="dc34a-104">Det här dokumentet förklarar hur du anpassar olika infrastrukturinställningarna och infrastrukturen uppgradera princip för Service Fabric-klustret.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-104">This document tells you how to customize the various fabric settings and the fabric upgrade policy for your Service Fabric cluster.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-105">Du kan anpassa dem på portalen eller med en Azure Resource Manager-mall.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-105">You can customize them on the portal or using an Azure Resource Manager template.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-106">Inte alla inställningar kan vara tillgängliga via portalen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-106">Not all settings may be available via the portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-107">Anpassa den med hjälp av en Azure Resource Manager-mall om en inställning nedan inte är tillgängliga via portalen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-107">In case a setting listed below is not available via the portal customize it using an Azure Resource Manager template.</span></span>
> 

## <a name="customizing-service-fabric-cluster-settings-using-azure-resource-manager-templates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dc34a-108">Anpassa inställningar för Service Fabric-kluster med hjälp av Azure Resource Manager-mallar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-108">Customizing Service Fabric cluster settings using Azure Resource Manager templates</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="dc34a-109">Stegen nedan illustrerar hur du lägger till en ny inställning *MaxDiskQuotaInMB* till den *diagnostik* avsnitt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-109">The steps below illustrate how to add a new setting *MaxDiskQuotaInMB* to the *Diagnostics* section.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-110">Gå till https://resources.azure.com</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-110">Go to https://resources.azure.com</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-111">Navigera till din prenumeration genom att expandera prenumerationer -> resurs grupper -> Microsoft.ServiceFabric -> klustrets namn</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-111">Navigate to your subscription by expanding subscriptions -> resource groups -> Microsoft.ServiceFabric -> Your Cluster Name</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-112">I det övre högra hörnet väljer du ”full”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-112">In the top right corner, select "Read/Write"</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-113">Välj Redigera och uppdatera den `fabricSettings` JSON-element och lägga till ett nytt element</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-113">Select Edit and update the `fabricSettings` JSON element and add a new element</span></span>

```
      {
        "name": "Diagnostics",
        "parameters": [
          {
            "name": "MaxDiskQuotaInMB",
            "value": "65536"
          }
        ]
      }
```

### <a name="section-name-transactionalreplicator"></a><span data-ttu-id="dc34a-203">Avsnittsnamn: TransactionalReplicator</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-203">Section Name: TransactionalReplicator</span></span>
| <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-204">**Parametern**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-204">**Parameter**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-205">**Tillåtna värden**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-205">**Allowed Values**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="dc34a-206">**Vägledning eller en kort beskrivning**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc34a-206">**Guidance or short Description**</span></span> |
